+  19 from flask_login import login_required, current_user
+  20 from sqlalchemy.exc import SQLAlchemyError
+  21
+  22 from src.extensions import db
+  23 from src.models.survey import Survey, SurveyOption, SurveyResponse
+  24
+  25 survey_bp = Blueprint('survey', __name__, url_prefix='/api/surveys')
+  26
+  27
+  28 @survey_bp.route('/', methods=['GET'])
+  29 @login_required
+  30 def get_surveys():
+  31     """Get all surveys for the current user."""
+  32     try:
+  33         surveys = Survey.query.filter_by(user_id=current_user.user_id).all()
+  34         return jsonify({
+  35             'surveys': [survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys]
+  36         }), 200
+  37     except Exception as e:
+  38         current_app.logger.error(f"Error retrieving surveys: {str(e)}")
+  39         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to retrieve surveys'}), 500
+  40
+  41
+  42 @survey_bp.route('/<int:survey_id>', methods=['GET'])
+  43 @login_required
+  44 def get_survey(survey_id):
+  45     """Get a specific survey."""
+  46     try:
+  47         survey = Survey.query.filter_by(survey_id=survey_id, user_id=current_user.user_id).first()
+  48         if not survey:
+  49             return jsonify({'error': 'Survey not found'}), 404
+  50
+  51         return jsonify(survey.to_dict()), 200
+  52     except Exception as e:
+  53         current_app.logger.error(f"Error retrieving survey: {str(e)}")
+  54         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to retrieve survey'}), 500
+  55
+  56
+  57 @survey_bp.route('/', methods=['POST'])
+  58 @login_required
+  59 def create_survey():
+  60     """Create a new survey."""
+  61     data = request.get_json()
+  62
+  63     # Validate input
+  64     if not data or not data.get('title'):
+  65         return jsonify({'error': 'Survey title is required'}), 400
+  66
+  67     options = data.get('options', [])
+  68     if len(options) < 2 or len(options) > 5:
+  69         return jsonify({'error': 'Survey must have between 2 and 5 options'}), 400
+  70
+  71     try:
+  72         # Create survey
+  73         survey = Survey(
+  74             user_id=current_user.user_id,
+  75             title=data['title'],
+  76             description=data.get('description')
+  77         )
+  78         db.session.add(survey)
+  79         db.session.flush()  # Get survey_id without committing
+  80
+  81         # Add options
+  82         for i, option_text in enumerate(options, 1):
+  83             option = SurveyOption(
+  84                 survey_id=survey.survey_id,
+  85                 option_text=option_text,
+  86                 option_order=i
+  87             )
+  88             db.session.add(option)
+  89
+  90         db.session.commit()
+  91         return jsonify({
+  92             'message': 'Survey created successfully',
+  93             'survey': survey.to_dict()
+  94         }), 201
+  95     except SQLAlchemyError as e:
+  96         db.session.rollback()
+  97         current_app.logger.error(f"Database error creating survey: {str(e)}")
+  98         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to create survey'}), 500
+  99     except Exception as e:
+ 100         db.session.rollback()
+ 101         current_app.logger.error(f"Error creating survey: {str(e)}")
+ 102         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to create survey'}), 500
+ 103
+ 104
+ 105 @survey_bp.route('/<int:survey_id>', methods=['PUT'])
+ 106 @login_required
+ 107 def update_survey(survey_id):
+ 108     """Update a survey."""
+ 109     data = request.get_json()
+ 110
+ 111     if not data:
+ 112         return jsonify({'error': 'No data provided'}), 400
+ 113
+ 114     try:
+ 115         survey = Survey.query.filter_by(survey_id=survey_id, user_id=current_user.user_id).first()
+ 116         if not survey:
+ 117             return jsonify({'error': 'Survey not found'}), 404
+ 118
+ 119         # Update survey fields
+ 120         if 'title' in data:
+ 121             survey.title = data['title']
+ 122         if 'description' in data:
+ 123             survey.description = data['description']
+ 124         if 'is_active' in data:
+ 125             survey.is_active = data['is_active']
+ 126
+ 127         db.session.commit()
+ 128         return jsonify({
+ 129             'message': 'Survey updated successfully',
+ 130             'survey': survey.to_dict()
+ 131         }), 200
+ 132     except Exception as e:
+ 133         db.session.rollback()
+ 134         current_app.logger.error(f"Error updating survey: {str(e)}")
+ 135         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to update survey'}), 500
+ 136
+ 137
+ 138 @survey_bp.route('/<int:survey_id>', methods=['DELETE'])
+ 139 @login_required
+ 140 def delete_survey(survey_id):
+ 141     """Delete a survey."""
+ 142     try:
+ 143         survey = Survey.query.filter_by(survey_id=survey_id, user_id=current_user.user_id).first()
+ 144         if not survey:
+ 145             return jsonify({'error': 'Survey not found'}), 404
+ 146
+ 147         db.session.delete(survey)
+ 148         db.session.commit()
+ 149         return jsonify({'message': 'Survey deleted successfully'}), 200
+ 150     except Exception as e:
+ 151         db.session.rollback()
+ 152         current_app.logger.error(f"Error deleting survey: {str(e)}")
+ 153         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to delete survey'}), 500
+ 154
+ 155
+ 156 @survey_bp.route('/<int:survey_id>/respond', methods=['POST'])
+ 157 def submit_response(survey_id):
+ 158     """Submit a response to a survey."""
+ 159     data = request.get_json()
+ 160
+ 161     # Validate input
+ 162     if not data or not data.get('option_id'):
+ 163         return jsonify({'error': 'Option ID is required'}), 400
+ 164
+ 165     try:
+ 166         # Check if survey exists and is active
+ 167         survey = Survey.query.filter_by(survey_id=survey_id, is_active=True).first()
+ 168         if not survey:
+ 169             return jsonify({'error': 'Survey not found or inactive'}), 404
+ 170
+ 171         # Check if option belongs to the survey
+ 172         option = SurveyOption.query.filter_by(
+ 173             option_id=data['option_id'],
+ 174             survey_id=survey_id
+ 175         ).first()
+ 176         if not option:
+ 177             return jsonify({'error': 'Invalid option for this survey'}), 400
+ 178
+ 179         # Create response
+ 180         response = SurveyResponse(
+ 181             survey_id=survey_id,
+ 182             option_id=data['option_id'],
+ 183             respondent_email=data.get('email')
+ 184         )
+ 185         db.session.add(response)
+ 186         db.session.commit()
+ 187
+ 188         return jsonify({
+ 189             'message': 'Response submitted successfully',
+ 190             'response_id': response.response_id
+ 191         }), 201
+ 192     except Exception as e:
+ 193         db.session.rollback()
+ 194         current_app.logger.error(f"Error submitting response: {str(e)}")
+ 195         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to submit response'}), 500
+ 196
+ 197
+ 198 @survey_bp.route('/<int:survey_id>/results', methods=['GET'])
+ 199 @login_required
+ 200 def get_results(survey_id):
+ 201     """Get results for a survey."""
+ 202     try:
+ 203         # Check if survey belongs to current user
+ 204         survey = Survey.query.filter_by(survey_id=survey_id, user_id=current_user.user_id).first()
+ 205         if not survey:
+ 206             return jsonify({'error': 'Survey not found'}), 404
+ 207
+ 208         # Get all options for this survey
+ 209         options = SurveyOption.query.filter_by(survey_id=survey_id).all()
+ 210
+ 211         # Count responses for each option
+ 212         results = {}
+ 213         total_responses = 0
+ 214
+ 215         for option in options:
+ 216             count = SurveyResponse.query.filter_by(option_id=option.option_id).count()
+ 217             results[option.option_text] = count
+ 218             total_responses += count
+ 219
+ 220         return jsonify({
+ 221             'survey_title': survey.title,
+ 222             'total_responses': total_responses,
+ 223             'results': results
+ 224         }), 200
+ 225     except Exception as e:
+ 226         current_app.logger.error(f"Error retrieving results: {str(e)}")
+ 227         return jsonify({'error': 'Failed to retrieve results'}), 500
